Mr. Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Our Responsibility
I would like to express my gratitude for the hard work you have done in your local areas. 
Today, I will speak under the title 'Our Responsibility.' 
What kind of being am I with a certain mission?
You are well aware that, although you have gathered here for a reason, we possess content that is different from that of the people of the world, especially considering our current situation. 
We are not a group that has gathered around the national ideology that any one country has claimed until now. We are a group gathered by a new providence that has never existed in any era of history. You must always be aware of this. 
When viewed from the perspective of an individual, I am one person among the citizens of the Republic of Korea, but when viewed against the backdrop of the overall providential will, I am different from individuals who have gone through a life journey centered on themselves. My individual existence is one that is attached to the will of providence. In other words, because I stand on a foundation that includes the content of God's providence that has traversed through historical eras, even though my position is that of an individual, that foundation is connected to the will of providence that moves the entirety of history. 
This was said on Saturday, August 29, 1970, at the Central Training Center (Sutaek-ri).
This speech was given during the second general assembly of the Heart of Faith Association.
8   Our Responsibility
Therefore, you are not just a mere teenager around the age of 20, but an individual who can take on a historical mission. You must realize this. 
From this perspective, we, who stand in this position, are not merely beings focused on the mission of this era, but individuals who are to make decisions regarding the providential content that will be left for the future era we will face. Therefore, you must understand that your existence is not a private one, whether you go left or right, or forward or backward; it is a historical and public existence. 
Our Unification Church must gather all such providential content and present a new direction, establishing a foundation of tradition that is not ashamed to represent any era of the past, present, or future. You must understand that this is the mission of the Unification Church. When considering that we stand in such a position, and that I myself stand in such a position, this is indeed a serious matter. 
Then, what is the destination that our Unification Church must pursue through the historical era? We must not be confined to the boundaries of religion or belong to any one denomination. We must transcend this. We must go beyond the current global ideologies and reach a world that must ultimately be achieved through those ideologies. This responsibility lies with our Unification Church, and you must recognize that it exists on the stage where we are active. 
From this standpoint, today, we are individuals who are citizens of the limited Republic of Korea, members of a certain school, or members of a local church, but we must not be limited to just being people who belong within those boundaries. We must be individuals with the subjectivity to manage those boundaries from a position that transcends them. We must become a Unification Church of that nature, and you must realize that you must become individuals of that nature. 
When we talk about our responsibility, of course, there is the responsibility of the entire Unification Church and the responsibility of each individual, but the departments of that responsibility will manifest in various forms. 
9 
The issue is how to align our direction of activity with the will
Some of you may be attending university, while others may be on the front lines representing this nation, fighting from a sacrificial position. While there may be various directions depending on the individual, the direction itself is not the problem. The issue is how to unify that direction with the will. This is a responsibility that you must take on. 
This mission remains unchanged. 
No matter how much the environment changes, you must not be absorbed by that changing environment; rather, you must possess the subjective capacity to absorb that environment. Without this, you cannot claim to have fulfilled your responsibility as one called by the providential will that has emerged through history. 
Regardless of what kind of environment you find yourself in or what diverse directions you may take, you must not be absorbed by them; instead, you must solidify your own position to block them and present a new image and new purpose that can influence them. This is indeed a significant responsibility that we must pledge to uphold. 
Your position must not be detached from the whole; it must always be a position that maintains a relationship with the whole. In both horizontal and vertical relationships, you must have a relationship that can correspond and support each other. Through this, you can develop the current foundation of the church itself. Furthermore, the church must not only develop as a church but must also encompass individuals with intrinsic personalities who can connect with various fields of society, enabling them to become part of society. Additionally, when moving for the sake of the church itself, you must gather and mobilize individuals from various directions. 
From this perspective, even though each of you may be in diverse positions within the church, you must approach the goal with a single direction that is undoubtedly aligned with the purpose. 
10   Our Responsibility
Today, this gathering is called the Heart of Faith Association, right? We are now transitioning into the 1970s, and the 1960s and 1970s are different points in time. From this standpoint, what kind of new image will you present to the Unification Church as the newly established Heart of Faith Association? 
There has been a traditional direction that the church has pursued centered on the providential will until now. Even if the direction you will take in the future is different from that direction, it must ultimately align with the same purpose. You must go straight, but in order to expand the field of the will more broadly, you must stand laterally and traverse various angles of direction. 
Therefore, during this process of traversing such directions and distances, you may feel a sense of distance from the church, but after going through this process, you must ultimately align and unify with that traditional direction. Without taking on this responsibility, you will feel a sense of guilt in your faith life moving forward. In other words, while your comrades are on the front lines fighting, you may feel guilty as you pursue your studies. 
Thus, those attending university must regard that university as an extension of our activities. Whether one is active in the local area or studying at university, the positions are the same. You must carry the notion that you are in the same position in terms of developing and advancing towards a single purpose. 
The Goals of the Unification Church in the 1970s
So what is that goal? The goal is to unify the whole. Therefore, the purpose of that activity must not be limited to a specific university, such as Seoul National University or Korea University. The purpose must extend beyond the university realm and be directed towards the Republic of Korea. 
Those who work for the Unification Church must also work not only for the development of the Unification Church but must do so with the Republic of Korea as the standard. 
11 
They must have the conviction to foster our traditional ideology for the development of the Republic of Korea and to solidify the foundation for the development of the Republic of Korea. This is the same. In other words, the purpose is the same. 
To form a nation, the church alone is not sufficient. There are larger societal issues involved. Moreover, when considering many countries in the current era, even if sovereigns have established their own national perspectives based on historical traditions, they cannot carry out global policies based on that foundation. Instead, they are influenced by various global ideologies. 
At a time when we cannot absolutize the internal traditional ideology, we must also possess the capacity to absorb external foundations that can align with global ideologies. When considering this, we must always remember that we should not limit ourselves to the Republic of Korea but should aim for a higher dimension beyond the Republic of Korea. 
Today, whether you are studying at a university or working hard as an active member in a local area, you must think at a higher level that you are not just working for that locality but for the Republic of Korea and for the world. 
If the whole proceeds towards this higher point of convergence of purpose, it will develop its respective field as long as it remains unchanged. This is the position that the Unification Church requires in relation to the 1970s, and you must understand this. Therefore, while our church has previously engaged in unilateral activities centered on the church, it is now expanding into various activities. 
Then to what extent should this be developed in the future? It must develop beyond the departments that the Republic of Korea's government possesses. Without this, we cannot reach the global stage. When considering this issue, we can see that the path we are taking is not becoming narrower but is gradually expanding. Such an era is awaiting us. 
You must understand this. 
Establishing a Global Tradition and Sacrifice
Then, what does the teacher desire from you in your work for the church? It is to horizontally expand the traditional ideology that has been the core or has come down vertically, connecting it to all departments and developing it. This must be expanded further. To do this, there must be a center, and that center can be established through the church organization. The church must figure out how to unify the different paths that have diverged and find a point of agreement in ideological direction, and how to provide an unchanging ideological foundation for numerous church members and those working from different positions. 
This is why the teacher has emphasized establishing tradition until now. Establish tradition… That tradition must not only be the tradition of the church. The tradition established by the church must become the tradition of the entire society, and that society's tradition must become the tradition of the nation, and that nation's tradition must become the tradition of the world. 
What this means is that the tradition must align with the historical tradition of God, who has been guiding providence for 6,000 years. That historical tradition transcends time. Only when established in such a tradition can we embark on a new tradition in the future. How to create such a tradition is an important issue. 
So how do we create such a tradition? That tradition must be one that can overcome any trials and sufferings. Furthermore, that tradition must not be led by the nation but must lead the nation, and it must not be led by the world but must be able to lead the world. 
From this standpoint, what must be the subject? The foundation centered on the content of this traditional providence must be the subject. Only then can we unify the nation in one direction and unify the world in one direction. Such a tradition is steadfast, and in establishing such a tradition, there must be a strong ideological foundation that can support all members both spiritually and physically. 
Considering this issue, you who must establish that tradition must not be people who wish for personal success centered on society. You must be individuals who can resolve to become a stepping stone for the nation and to sacrifice yourselves for the world. 
So where should you sacrifice? There will be various levels of sacrifice. There are places where one can sacrifice as an individual, as a family, as a tribe, as a nation, and as a world. Among these, where should the sacrifice be made? Anyone living on this earth would want to sacrifice for the world. 
However, for global sacrifice to stand on a traditional foundation, it must be based on national sacrifice. Furthermore, to support national sacrifice, there must be a foundation of ethnic sacrifice, and ethnic sacrifice must be based on tribal sacrifice, tribal sacrifice must be based on familial sacrifice, and familial sacrifice must be based on individual sacrifice. 
Without this traditional foundation of sacrifice, no matter how much one establishes a global tradition, it cannot be a tradition that can be presented before any nation, and no matter how much one establishes a national tradition, it cannot be a tradition that can be presented before the ethnicity. Moreover, no matter how much one establishes a tradition centered on the ethnicity, it cannot be a tradition that can be presented before any specific tribe, and even if one presents that tradition as a tradition for the tribe, it cannot be presented without the content of familial tradition. Additionally, to establish a family tradition, one must have the content of individual tradition. 
What should individuals, families, tribes, ethnicities, nations, and the world that must establish such a tradition do for future generations? They must live with global thought and global will. 
14   Our Responsibility
To live with the will and to go along with the will, one must overcome the path of personal suffering, as well as the path of familial suffering. Additionally, one must overcome the paths of tribal, ethnic, national, and global suffering. One must recognize that overcoming such paths of suffering is an obligation that one must fulfill and must proceed with a historical resolution that says, "I must do it." Without such a foundation of sacrifice, the foundation of tradition cannot be established.
is something that cannot be polished.  
One must have the awareness of being a representative of history.  
What is human desire? If you ask what your desire is, what your hope is, everyone would answer that it is to conquer the world. Everyone wants to make the world their own. But can you make the world your own all at once? To make the world your own, you must first make one country your own. And to make one country your own, you need the support of its people.  
However, the support of the people cannot be obtained immediately. First, you must gain the support of your own tribe. And even to gain the support of that tribe, you cannot obtain it immediately; you must become a person who is supported within your family. And to gain the support of that family, you must become a central figure that the entire family can look up to.  
How do you become that central figure? From the individual to the family, tribe, nation, and world, you must be recognized as someone who sacrifices for the whole. However, the sacrifice of the individual should not be just personal; it must be centered around a historical worldview. The worldview that has emerged through providential history until now, even though it has not yet been fully realized, requires sacrifice to find that worldview.  
From this perspective, my individual self must have the awareness of being a representative of this historical era. If we cut history centered around people in their twenties like you, you are the responsible party in this historical era. In other words, countless prophets have passed through, but those prophets came hoping for you. Thus, you, who are the embodiment of hope, are not just a being for the Republic of Korea today. You are a being of hope for the world. You must become an individual who has this awareness and become the embodiment of historical hope. You must become a global entity, not just a national one.  
As a being of global hope representing this historical era, you are not limited to the Republic of Korea. You must have the awareness that you emerge as a global prodigy in the history of God's providence, that is, in the history of God's restoration providence aimed at saving humanity. You must become someone who can achieve that.  
To bear historical fruit,  
You are historical figures. When you pray, the phrase "the fruit of six thousand years" carries that meaning. It is not nationalistic. It is not limited to the Republic of Korea. It is global. However, from a position that has a higher dimension than the global, one who can inherit history is someone who becomes an embodiment of historical hope. That hope is not personal; it is global. From there, the world unfolds. You must establish a traditional foundation from that standpoint to say that you have established a tradition for the world. If you cannot stand in that position, you cannot be called a being of hope.  
So you must live. You must live your life with dedication. When we look at life laterally, it connects everything from the family to the world, forming a circle. To draw a circle, there must be a center, and to be that center, what must you do? To make it revolve, the center must be stronger. According to the principle of strength, when comparing centripetal and centrifugal forces, if the centrifugal force is strong, the center is pulled away. Therefore, to avoid being pulled away and to remain in a state of rest, the center must be strong. If it is strong, it will not be pulled away.  
Today's world is pulling me in. However, you must become a center that pulls the world toward you rather than being pulled away. Such a person does not live for themselves. They live for the world. Therefore, you must have a thorough mindset that says, "From now on, I will live my entire life for the world." "I will pioneer for that, fight for that, and strive for that. Everything about me starts from that and ends with that!" You must establish that tradition.  
Then, how can you show that you can establish such a tradition? It cannot be just words. It must be shown in a way that anyone can verify. So where will you go? "In my journey, I will abandon this and that and start from this global foundation." Can you do that? No, you cannot. If that happens, who will cultivate the tradition of this foundation? In short, it will break. No one can bypass the starting point.  
The reason why philosophy has not been able to clarify all fundamental human problems until now is that it has not excavated the traditional origins of human life. Humans have a stronger desire for life than for death. There is nothing stronger than the desire for life. Humans must be alive to have hope. Among human desires, the desire for life is the strongest. Therefore, without establishing the origin of that life, one cannot establish the tradition of life.  
From that perspective, the Unification Church must emerge with a worldview based on the tradition of life. Did the Unification Church start with such a worldview? Yes, it did. It started centered around God. Even though it has gone through six thousand years of history, even at this moment, that motivation still governs human vitality.  
However, I must be able to say that I, who possess life force, govern history, and that history does not govern me, in order to become the fruit of historical hope and the focal point of historical hope. But if I cannot do that and am consumed by history, dominated by history, and absorbed by history, how can I become a historical fruit? If that happens, I will flow along with history.  
A strong tradition must be established to act in the 1970s.  
That is why a core tradition, like an atom, must be established. The nucleus has tremendous power. The atomic nucleus itself is not light. It has a more powerful subjective force, capable of absorbing all relative existences. Because it can not only absorb but also digest and propel, the nucleus persists.  
In the same way, our Unification Church must establish such a powerful tradition. That tradition is not the one you want to create. It must be a tradition that is aware of history, resolute in the present age, and can present new purposes for the future.  
So how can we become such a nucleus? We must strengthen ourselves. To unite strongly, we must push strongly. When you go to a large automobile factory, you can see that when making parts, they place iron plates on a required mold and press them with a press weighing thousands of tons to obtain the desired shape. You must have that kind of strength as well. Without it, you cannot be solidified.  
In that sense, in the 1970s, we must establish the traditional thought of the Unification Church. Without establishing this tradition, even if we develop, it will be like a boastful claim. It will be like fruit without seeds. That is why we have emphasized tradition until now. Since that tradition is a historical tradition, it is not one that any era can dominate.  
So what is the core of the tradition that can dominate the historical era? It is neither today's Republic of Korea nor the current world. It is the country and world that will come in the future. Who will bring about this future country and world? It must be achieved through me, through us.  
When there is a war, if the strong and the weak fight, the weak will retreat before the strong. The weak cannot help but yield to the strong. In doing so, the yielding weak becomes the fertilizer for the strong. They become the elements of life absorbed by the strong. Do you understand what I mean? Any country develops in that way. The history of cultural development or the history of religious development has also gone through such processes. In other words, higher religions absorb lower religions. When they compete for superiority but lack the ability and have to surrender, they are absorbed by the other.  
God's strategy and Satan's strategy  
The Unification Church has fought such battles centered around the Republic of Korea until now. Even now, a fierce battle is ongoing. Behind the scenes, fierce struggles are taking place that you do not know about. A duel is unfolding to determine the weak and the strong. In that battle, only one victor will remain.  
God works to make the person standing on the foundation that contributes to His will victorious, while Satan works to make the person in an evil position victorious. God proceeds with an unchanging strategy from a true position, while Satan uses deceptive tactics to disguise falsehood as truth to temporarily evade weaknesses. Therefore, even if falsehood occupies the position of truth, it cannot last long. From within itself, contradictions arise and digest it. Thus, it develops into another system. When that happens, God again governs based on that system.  
The one who strikes will inevitably be struck back, so even if evil seems to have triumphed over good, that evil will eventually be met with its own downfall. From there, it will rapidly decline. Thus, within three generations, it will return to a new angle, according to the principle.  
Looking at the communist world, it has fallen from a global communist realm to a national communist realm. If communism is centered around China, it will split into right-wing and left-wing communism, and then communism will remain only in form, becoming insignificant. At that time, if a philosophical system capable of absorbing it emerges, it can absorb communism in an instant. That is why we must create a strong core tradition.  
In that sense, today, the Unification Church must be stronger than it was in the 1960s. To do so, one should not try to establish a tradition by eating better, dressing better, and living better than others. If that is the case, it cannot become a tradition. Tradition is like solidifying the foundation of a house. If this is not firm and unshakeable, no matter how impressive a high-rise building you build, it will collapse in an instant. That is why the teacher advocates for establishing a strong tradition.  
A true loyalist emerges from individual character and educated family life.  
In this 1970s, we must lay the foundation of this tradition to pave the way to the world centered around the nation. That is why the teacher has been preparing for this since the late 1960s, which is the interdenominational movement and victory activities centered around our church.  
Therefore, from now on, wherever you go with the name of the Unification Church, you must live for the world. You must live for heaven and earth. Living for heaven and earth means living from a position of ownership. That position is guaranteed by history. The history of humanity that has passed through thousands of years can guarantee it, and the present age can guarantee it, and the future can guarantee it. Only by becoming a being standing on a solid foundation that can receive the guarantees of these three eras can you truly be called a son or daughter called by heaven as a worker of unification. From this standpoint, I truly envy the young men and women.  
Then, what will you sacrifice for? Regardless of who it is, you will want to sacrifice for something higher and be loyal to your country. However, a loyalist who is loyal to the country does not emerge immediately. It comes from the family, from the individual's character. In other words, it emerges from the character of oneself and the family life centered on education.  
Thus, through social activities, one enters a position that can influence the dignity of the nation. Based on such a foundation, one must stand in a position needed by the country; without that foundation, one can only become a flatterer or a sycophant.  
Where should the foundation of responsibility and tradition be placed?  
When we look at the issue of our responsibility, where should that responsible foundation be placed? Should it be placed on your own success? Should you think that since the Unification Church seems to have a global stage and can develop, you will use the Unification Church to achieve your own success? The Unification Church will never be used. Rather, if you are used, it will be you who is used, not the Unification Church.  
Where should that foundation be placed? Should it be placed on you as an individual? There cannot be a religion centered around the individual. Such a religion will perish. Should it be placed on your family? If a religion is centered around a family, when that family falls, that religion will also fall. If it is placed on a tribe, when that tribe falls, it will fall as well. If it is placed on a nation, when that nation falls, it will fall together.  
In other words, when you realize that today’s world cannot be guaranteed before heaven, that the nation cannot be guaranteed before heaven, and that the entire nation or society cannot be guaranteed before heaven, it will perish. If you place your foundation in a world that is destined to perish, it will also perish.  
Therefore, the question is where to place the foundation. If you place it in today’s Republic of Korea, if the Republic of Korea falls, you will fall with it. If you place it in communism, if communism falls, you will fall with it.  
Then what will not perish? This is the question. When we look at this issue, since God will not perish, we must place our foundation on the will that God desires. What is that will? It is to establish the world that God desires. Therefore, we must place our foundation on those who can govern and love that world.  
From that perspective, today, the Unification Church, which is emerging as a higher standard of thought aligned with God's providence, is something that everyone cannot help but admire.  
If your purpose for studying is for personal success, when the social conditions become such that individuals cannot succeed, you will enter a position of struggle within that society. Such a person is one who obstructs the welfare of the nation for the sake of their own family and forgets the public interest of the nation for their own benefit. Such a person is selling out their country.  
So where will you place the traditional foundation of your life, the traditional foundation of your living, and the traditional foundation of your hope? This is the question.  
The true purpose of life  
Among the young people of the Unification Church today, there are those who have come to the Unification Church because they believe in a man or woman who holds the Unification Church's ideology and want to meet such a partner. Such people are truly trivial.  
Such a person is less than a flying fly. A fly at least carries a smell, but what can such a person do? What can they become? What kind of spirit will they become?  
The reason the teacher has continued to fight throughout his life without getting tired is because of the conviction that he will die only after seeing that day. He wishes to see that day as soon as possible.
Because there is a purpose in life that must be shortened. Therefore, when the teacher wastes even an hour, he feels regret and repentance. In such situations, there is no room for fatigue or anything else. That is why the teacher has not yet become weary. He does not go back and forth. 

When you stand in a position centered on your purpose, where is the limit of that purpose? Is it for individual happiness? No. Is it for family happiness? No. You cannot center on individuals, families, tribes, nations, or states and achieve globalization. Those cannot drive globalization. We cannot leave aside the globalization movement that God desires, the ideal of heaven that God wishes, so we practice, train, and prepare to fulfill that purpose. If there are those among you living such a life, even if told to go elsewhere, they cannot leave. 

Even with a little experience in that, you will realize that there is no greater reward. Living such a life may seem like it will fail, but it does not; it may seem like it will break, but it does not. Even if the surrounding environment tries to ruin me, it absolutely cannot. It may seem like it will end, but it does not; it may seem like it will fail, but it endures. You may not have had such experiences. That is why you will fail if you go alone. Do you understand what I mean? 

You must realize that you are necessary in carrying out that purpose alongside the protagonists of the world, the universe, and history. You must recognize that your individual existence is needed to fulfill a historical mission and live your life accordingly. Life is the journey of a lifetime, and living is the journey of a day. A thorough ideology regarding that life and a thorough affinity in practical aspects should become the purpose of your life in overcoming and breaking through that environment. 

The question is whether you stand on the foundation of true tradition. Because of this content, God demands such people, and by becoming such a person, God establishes and works through me. However, if one cannot become such a person, God will move on. 

So where did the Unification Church start from? Raise your hand if you have been in the Unification Church for 7 years. There are some. Now raise your hand if you have been here for more than 5 years. There are many. It will continue to increase. So, has the person who has been a member for 7 years walked straight toward God from the very beginning of that 7-year period? How have they walked? You must not lose your direction. If you have worried God while going around in circles to follow the purpose, what good is it after 7 years? If the person who was evangelized was someone who wandered without direction, they will lead everyone to ruin. 

A couple who longed for a son should not just be happy about having a son. They must worry about how to raise that son to be a valuable person. A person who loves that son while worrying about such things is someone who understands the greater picture. However, if they are just happy about having a son without any such worries, they are starting off on the wrong foot. They should be able to worry about how to raise that son to be someone needed by the country. If they wanted a son to raise him as such, that means they started with the condition of starting for the country. This is an important issue. 

Are you now standing in the position of God's sons and daughters with traditional content? If you have such a tradition, it does not matter which direction you go. It is fine to go east or west. Since it spreads horizontally, it becomes a foundation for horizontal development. Such a person goes in the direction of the world of purpose, no matter where they go. 

Such a person can go to school or work. It does not matter if they go to college. Even if they go to college, if their center is intact, they can go toward the purpose from there. They can also go in the direction of the purpose while working. The forms may seem slightly different, but in terms of going toward the purpose, they are not different. It may seem like they are not going straight but going around, but that is not the case. 

You must have a thorough ideology centered on the purpose. Among our young students, there are those who fall out when they go to the military, and such people are better off falling out. The teacher does not try to rehabilitate such people. It is better to evangelize new people and help them make a decision than to rehabilitate such people. Those who fell out may have made a decision, but they are people who could not keep their decision before going to the military. That is why tradition is necessary. It is not that many people are needed, but that people who can establish tradition are needed. The question is how to establish someone who can represent the north, south, east, and west. 

What kind of foundation will you lay? The teacher himself has lived to lay a foundation until now. What I have lived until now is not just my own life. I know that my life will become an object of reverence for countless people who follow the Unification Church and this ideology and will become a standard for analysis and criticism, so I struggle to avoid paths that would burden my conscience or go against heavenly principles. 

Because that foundation is global, to find God's world, you must inevitably go through someone with such a global foundation. This path must go through me. You cannot go without passing through me. God works through people, so He cannot bypass my family. He cannot bypass my tribe or my nation. Therefore, such an individual must become such a family, and that family must foster such a tribe, and that tribe must create such a nation, and that nation must form such a world. 

To establish the unification ideology centered on the nation, your national perspectives must all align. But are you doing that now? A person who studies for their own success and gets a job to solve their own living problems is someone who will inevitably drift away from there. Therefore, even if you are going in different directions, you must have a thorough ideology regarding the standard of purpose. If you have that mindset, no one can infringe upon it. 

Thus, the question is whether you are aware that you can stand in such a traditional position with absolute authority. This awareness is with the world and with the times. Thus, no matter what era you are in, you will not be infringed upon by that era; rather, you will become the center of that era, digest it, and become someone who can recreate the world. God cannot help but be with such a person. 

When you stand in a lonely place for the purpose, God will be with you. Even if you stand alone in a lonely place, you are not standing there alone. When you stand in such a place, you must feel that God is working through this pitiful person. Why have Abel's been suffering in silence until now? 
August 29, 1970 (Saturday), at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).
* This message was given to the women evangelists who returned after completing a 40-day summer evangelism from July 20 to August 29, 1970, and the title was added by the editor. The beginning part was not recorded.

Now, let’s talk about the principle. Are you Abel or Cain? "We are Abel." Raise your hand if you think you are Abel. Until now, the principle has not clearly explained about Abel, but it will be clearly explained from now on.

Why do Christians who believe in Jesus suffer so much? In the language of the Unification Church, they talk about indemnity and restoration, but they can't even hit their enemies or curse them once. What is that? Doesn't that feel bad? The teacher has often felt angry while walking this path. How impatient is the teacher's personality? There have been many times when I wanted to cut off someone's head with a sword in one blow. Yet, I live as if I were dead. Why do I live like that? Why do you live like that? Let’s think about why we have to do that.

The teacher has confidence that wherever he goes, he can build a foundation that does not fall behind anyone. But why do we live like this? Why do we remain silent even when we are insulted and go through all sorts of things? And why do I tell those who have suffered until now to suffer more? Isn’t there anyone who would say such a thing? Isn’t that strange? You are thinking, "When will this end? The Unification Church, oh the Unification Church…." Haven't you thought like that? Is the Unification Church a foolish church?

What is the Unification Church trying to do? It is a church that aims to live according to the principles. The Unification Church is about living according to the principles of heaven. Then, is living according to the principles of heaven suffering? After sacrificing and suffering so much, isn't it enough? Now, what is this? You thought that being blessed would mean living well, but now you have to carry the burden of blessings and suffer again. What kind of blessing is that? 

Don’t you have any complaints? Have you complained, or not? "We have not complained." You probably don’t know how to complain because you lack content.

Let’s think about Jesus. Was Jesus good or not? "He was good." He was good before God, but before the world, he was not good. Before the world, he was not good. If you try to be good in both places, you can easily become neither this nor that. You must understand that. Jesus was good before God but not good before the world. How much was he not good? He was so not good that he died.

How not good was Jesus? Was it because he did something bad? No. He was good, but he was too good to be compared with them, which made him appear to do bad things. It was not that he did bad things because he was not good, but because he could not compare with them, he was seen as doing bad things. This is not found in the principles. 

The reason we must love Cain (the enemy) 
Before God created Adam, He loved the archangel. But when Adam was created...
After you have ascended, it means that you loved the archangel even more. You must clearly understand why Christianity teaches to love your enemies. Why did Jesus, at the moment of bleeding and dying on the cross, say, "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they are doing"? What does that mean? What on earth does it mean?

God loved the archangel. But has any human ever loved the archangel? Has there ever been a person who loved the archangel as God loved him? Was there such a person? "No, there wasn't."

To inherit from parents, one must be in harmony with their heart. Then, actions must align as well. The child who receives the most love from parents is the one who is favored by them. And the child who has captured the parents' love. Next, it is the child who aligns their actions with those of the parents, the child who shares the same will as the parents, and the child who has the same hopes as the parents. No matter how many sons there are, it is the child who comes closest to those standards who inherits from the parents. Isn't that right?

Has any human ever loved the angel that God loves? They have not. Then who is Adam? He is the son of God. He is in a father-son relationship with God. Therefore, they must be of one heart and mind. Thus, if the Father loves the archangel, the Son must also love him.

So, in what position did humans fall? They fell from the position of not being able to love the archangel as an angel should be loved. Therefore, this must be restored. Why has God been slandered by the archangel, the beast of evil, for 6,000 years? Is God so great? If He just kicked that wicked being away, it would be over, but why has He accepted Satan's slander by saying, "Yes, you are right"? It is because there is a principle that requires love for the archangel, and it is necessary to establish the condition that the Son of God came and loved the archangel. Until that time, we cannot say that God and humans have fulfilled their responsibilities. Because this standard remains, God must also love Satan, and humans must also love Satan. Therefore, Cain is the representative of the archangel, and Abel is the representative of God.

Then why did we say to love the archangel, that is, the enemy? It is because fallen humans cannot return to God, to the original world, without loving the archangel. From God's providential viewpoint, the archangel is Satan and the enemy, but in order to correct that Satan fundamentally, the Son of God must love him just as God loves him. Because of this principle, we must love him. Otherwise, we cannot inherit all that belongs to God.

In other words, unless there is harmony of heart, harmony of life, and harmony of desire with the Father, we cannot inherit all that belongs to the Father. If one is not like the Father, they cannot inherit. Since the Son cannot inherit unless he loves the archangel whom the Father loved, he must love him even if the archangel has become Satan. Otherwise, he cannot return to the position of the original human, so Abel, who stands in the position of Adam, must love Cain, who stands in the position of the archangel.

However, who is the archangel that humans must love? It must be the archangel who betrays God's will and tries to kill Adam, not the archangel who follows God's will and serves Adam and Eve. This is because one cannot return without loving even such a Satan. This is the path of restoration.

The reason Jesus prayed for his enemies was because of God's heavenly principle. Just as God loved the archangel based on this principle, Adam and Eve should have stood in such a position and loved the archangel, but they could not. Therefore, Jesus had to establish a standard of having loved the archangel at some point. Otherwise, there would be no way to return to the original position, so even as He was dying on the cross, Jesus prayed to forgive those who were enemies in order to establish the condition of having loved the enemy. We must understand that the content of His prayer for the enemy was fulfilled in this way. Do you understand what I mean?

To become Abel
A perfect son of God is an unfallen son. He is a son who receives God's love and loves God. Then, after loving God, whom should that son love? He must love the archangel. Only then can he become a perfect son of God.

What must we become in the age of restoration? We must become Abel. Then, how should we walk the path of restoration to return to God's world following Abel's way? Therefore, without entering that position and without becoming one with God, they could not love the archangel whom God loved. When we view love in this way, we conclude that Adam and Eve fell during their immature years.

What must Abel do? First, he must become one with God, and second, he must love the archangel. So, are you Abel or Cain? "I am Abel." Have you become Abel? To become Abel, you must receive God's love; are you receiving God's love? Do you see it that way?
