When asked which is better between the two, when distinguishing between good and bad, the issue is which has more valuable content. This is how we choose when selecting items. The same applies when dealing with people. Among friends, whom do you want to get close to or form a connection with? You tend to approach those who are more valuable, better, higher, and broader than yourself. Moreover, it is human nature to want to possess the qualities of those people through any means.

In this regard, God is the same. Just as we humans have the heart to align ourselves with what is more valuable when dealing with things or people, the God who created us humans is also the same. It goes without saying that God's love, wishes, and all intentions are focused on what is more valuable.

You, who are here, and the teachers are in the same position. However, we must also strive to be people of higher value, that is, people with broader, deeper, and higher content that all humanity demands. If there is such a person, we will want to get close to them, and God will also want to get close to that person. If God wants to be close and humans want to be close, we can understand that all things created for humanity cannot help but draw near to that person.

When viewed this way, it can be said that humans are the crown of creation. Then, how valuable must the central being who can serve as a model for all be? They must be an infinitely valuable being. If God exists, He must take that person who can serve as a model and unite with them. Therefore, that person must be a being who encompasses and exceeds absolute value.

When viewed this way, what kind of person is the one who can become a model with God and with all things and the universe? What is the ideal standard that such a true person desires, the lifestyle of that true person, the criteria that form the character of that true person, or the ideal internal elements that we humans desire? It is clear that it is not something sad.

A Model Position
Everyone dislikes sadness. Everyone wishes that difficulties do not relate to them. When we see a family going through hardship, we feel sympathy for that family. Sympathy means giving a part of oneself to them. If someone is unhappy, to move to a position where they are not unhappy, they must receive help from their surroundings to eliminate the conditions of their unhappiness. 

So, what is a truly happy position? It is a position where one can always give. It is not about giving sadness but about being able to give joy always. This is what everyone desires.

If there is a person who can be a model and the center of all, what kind of position will they occupy? It will not be a sad position. It will also not be an evil position. So, what kind of position will it be? It will be a true position, a joyful position. Furthermore, that position will be infinitely happy. That happiness must not be limited to finite boundaries but must be happiness from an infinite position. When asked if such a valuable person existed on this earth, the answer is that they did not.

What about Jesus, who came to this earth as the Son of God? Of course, even though He could be a model for all, He was in a position where He had to give because He was in a world of evil. Since the world Jesus faced was sad, He had to give all the time. After giving, His high position would lower. Even if a bucket of water is full, it decreases after pouring out. No matter how high Jesus' position was, when faced with a sad environment, He had to give. After giving, what happens? He cannot be in a joyful environment.

So, why could Jesus not stand in a position of joy? Because after giving, He would inevitably encounter difficult circumstances, and the content of joy would decrease. The issue is how to replenish that decrease. If He cannot replenish it, He will feel unspeakable unhappiness, unspeakable loneliness, and unspeakable hardship.

What is the only way to replenish what has been given? It is to comfort the sad person and unite with them, helping them rise from their sad position to a better one. If, after giving, one can receive back what they have given, they are a happy person. Happiness begins from there.

For example, if a sad person in a position of 100,000 rises to a position of 200,000 because of themselves, they may lose 10 of their own content, but that person gains 10. When this decrease is compensated, the 10 becomes developed because of oneself. When the phenomenon of development occurs centered on oneself rather than loss or decline, joy comes.

Also, just because one plans for something worth 1,000,000 does not mean it happens all at once. It happens gradually: 100,000 is achieved, then 200,000, and so on, until 1,000,000. As the possibilities of achieving what one hopes for increase, people feel joy. In this regard, the question is whether we can become people who can serve as a model, as the title of the message suggests.

Criteria for the Character of a Model
So, what is a model? What kind of person can be a model? A person who can elevate what is low and also stand in a position where they can elevate themselves. Otherwise, they cannot be a model. In other words, a person who can be a model is someone needed above and below, to the left and right, and in front and behind. They can support both sides. It is not just about supporting; it is about being in a position to receive back after giving support. If one cannot stand in such a position, they do not become a model.

The criteria for being a model are not limited to the East; they must also be a model in the West. Furthermore, they must not only be a model in the earthly world but also in the heavenly world. It is not about being a model for just a moment or in a specific environment; they must be a model representing the whole.

So, what kind of person can be a model? A person who influences others and does not suffer loss from that but rather receives more. In this regard, they must be connected to a higher value than we humans. Taking a tree as an example, a tree has roots, a trunk, and branches. The thick branches receive a lot of nutrients from the roots, allowing many branches to spread and many leaves to bloom. This is similar to how a thick branch appears as a central branch among others.

When you center yourselves and form connections with many people, they should be in a position where they can follow your model, aligning with you when you go left, right, forward, or backward. However, that cannot be the end. It must possess not only temporary content but also enduring content, standing in a position where it can influence the whole and also be influenced. When that happens, infinite development is inevitable. If a tree is in such a position, it is the same. Therefore, when the beings you interact with rise, you also receive relative influence, and your value as a being increases. When in such a position, true relationships will inevitably develop.

God desires you to be a source of comfort for sad people. We know that fallen humans live in an evil world and are in sadness. So, what should you, who live centered on the will, have to be a model before those who are sad? You cannot give joy without providing content that can comfort sadness. In other words, if the standard of the sad person is 10, if you fill them with a standard above that, such as 11, 12, or even 20, then that sad person will rejoice.

So, what should you prioritize in pushing forward the providence of heaven to remove this sadness? It is how close you are to God and how you can serve Him in a way that always brings Him joy. It must be that God rejoices because of you, not that God is saddened because of you. If God, who has felt greater loneliness and sorrow than any sadness I have felt, tries to replenish that, and if I can serve as a means to replenish that, then I must be an absolutely necessary person before God.

If you become a source of comfort for sad people, how valuable would that be? That is why it is said, "The kingdom is within your heart." The kingdom is not somewhere else; it is within my heart. A person who possesses the kingdom does not live in sadness but in joy. They do not pursue finite values but seek infinite values.

We are on a life journey with an end, but we do not live a life with an end; we live a life without end. In horizontal life, it does not end with horizontal living but must relate to deep vertical content. When deep vertical content influences the horizontal environment frequently, allowing that environment to shine, that person will inevitably become the center of life in that environment.

In this sense, to improve this sad world, the world of Satan, the evil world, we must give. Then, the question arises: do you have an infinite supply route to give? If there is a model, that model does not apply to just one place. It must be a standard that transcends all environments with absolute content. Therefore, you must draw a line centered on that and strive to shape it to align with it.

God also desires you to become a model person centered around you. The more evil the environment, the more it demands a person with such value. This is because the sad environment requires more of what can serve as a model.

When you become such a being and purify the environment, bringing joy to the central being, those in that environment can also rejoice around the model person. If today is more joyful than yesterday and tomorrow can be more joyful than today, if they can receive that content from the center, then they cannot help but be a model person before all humanity, whom God loves and with whom God can be with.

Externally monotonous, yet living a deep and high internal life, Jesus.
When we look at Jesus, His life was simple. For over 30 years, He lived as an assistant in the carpenter's household of Joseph, which was a very monotonous life. However, although He did not lead an externally changing life, beneath that simplicity, He possessed a complexity, breadth, and depth that allowed Him to overcome all His circumstances. This is why He could fill the path of suffering and loneliness with His profound inner life. He had the inner influence to not only alleviate His own suffering but also to bear the suffering of others, which is why God could not help but establish Him as a model for creating a new history. In other words, while Jesus led a simple external life, internally, He lived a complex, deep, and elevated life. You need to understand this.

Jesus' external life could not escape the limited environment of Joseph's household, nor could He break free from that workplace. Yet internally, He lived a life that transcended the household of Joseph, the nation of Israel, and the world, and even reached the heights of living in heaven. Because He led a life that could fill and overflow the external monotony, God had no choice but to recognize Jesus as a model human being. Therefore, God could not help but establish a relationship with Jesus and stand in a position to support Him. As a result, Jesus began with a worldview that was deep, broad, and high, which no one else could feel or realize.

So how did Jesus reach such a position? He did not only engage in external, horizontal living in His daily life but also pursued a vertical life to establish a deep relationship with God. You need to understand that He lived this dual life that no one else could. In other words, He did not merely live a life that could give but had a foundation to eternally receive that high and great value from God, which allowed Him to endure difficult and sorrowful circumstances.

When we become models
Our Unification Church members, when they first encountered the will upon entering the church, started with joy. They likely felt that everything in the world was centered around them. The more grace they received, the more they felt that everything was revived and related to them. Therefore, when they were joyful, they felt that all things rejoiced with them, and when they were sad, they felt that all things were sad together with them.

During such times, no matter how evil the world seemed, it did not appear evil, and no matter how sorrowful the world was, it did not seem sorrowful. They began to live with the hope of tomorrow and the commitment to tomorrow, seeing that joy could dwell in that sorrowful world. You may have experienced such moments in the past.

However, the standard of that time is different from now. It cannot help but be different. The sensations felt then were not flat sensations but three-dimensional sensations.

Even when dealing with people, many have experienced that their eyes became brighter in seeing the good points rather than the bad points, and their sensitivity to the good aspects became quicker than to the bad ones. Based on such a life, they should live centered around higher and broader content, yet in social and faith life, they are habitually repeating past behaviors. It is truly unfortunate that they have lost this discernment function.

When one is alone and enters a gracious position, they feel joy alone. Joy comes to them in a way that others cannot understand. There are times like the spring when all the plants bloom and emit fragrance. Or there are times in autumn when all the grains are ripening, longing for the owner's touch, and they feel the joy of harvesting. Those who do not have such moments are pitiful.

The closer one gets to God and the more they become one with Him, the more they become a person who can eternally be a model. When the day comes that the center of that model is determined, all existence will resonate with them and joyfully respond to them. Therefore, the closer one gets to such a position, even if the world is sorrowful, it does not appear sorrowful. Everything sorrowful that they face does not dominate them; rather, the joy that arises from transcending that sorrow governs them. Isn't such a position a place where one can be a model for humanity? Isn't such a place where one can possess heaven in their heart?

Everyone, there are many women here, but your own hearts must be such that you can lead your families to be like that. If you look at the world through green glasses, everything in the world will appear green. Good and bad results do not arise from the other party but manifest according to one's own heart. Therefore, you must be able to support and govern this.

To truly become a good person
From this perspective, what kind of person is a truly good person? A person who, when there is an evil person, picks apart their evil points and hates them as much as their evil exists is not a good person. A truly good person is one who can forget that evil and evaluate the value of goodness that resides within that evil as greater than the evil itself. Only then can they relate to that evil person from a good standpoint and guide them to a new position, presenting the conditions for happiness from that new standpoint. As a result, that person can take them as a model and form a relationship centered around them.

You must understand that if you stand in a position of cursing ‘evil’ itself because the other party is evil and evaluate that evil as worse than it is, there cannot be ‘good’ itself on this earth. Therefore, what kind of person is a good person? A good person loves even the evil person, and when facing a sorrowful person, they do not leave that sorrow as theirs but can feel it as their own sorrow. If they can enter that sorrowful position, alleviate that sorrow, and give their joy to that sorrowful person, then that person can be a model in any environment.

So how can one become such a person? They must transcend flat habits and notions. In other words, they should think, ‘I was born for that person, so I will become a sacrifice for them.’ They should also think, ‘I was born to make the evil person a good person.’ If one lives with the idea that they live for them, when difficult issues arise in that environment, they will not leave those issues as they are but will consider them their lifelong task and will seek to eliminate all evil and make it good.

To become good, one must not think of evil as someone else's but feel it as their own pain, staying up all night praying for them with tears and living with a heart that offers atonement for their sins. Such a person cannot help but become the central being of the evil person's nature.

Jesus Christ, who became a universal model
The person who stood in such a position was Jesus Christ. Jesus Christ is not only the savior of the age from a flat perspective but also the savior of the past through historical eras and the savior of the future. Therefore, when looking at all historical moments of humanity to come, one can see that past people had such sorrows, present people have such sorrows, and future people will have such sorrows, and He personally experienced the sorrows of humanity.

For such humanity, standing in the positions of both inner and outer centers, He understood and sympathized with them, considering all their difficulties as His own, shedding tears and struggling. Wasn't that Jesus Christ? We know that humanity strives to become one centered around such a person.

Therefore, what kind of person is a good person? A good person is one who sacrifices themselves to help others, forgives others, and when others are in difficulty, thinks of that difficulty as their own. We often call such a person a good person. It is our heart's desire to approach such a person; it is the path our hearts seek. When there is a model person, goodness develops through them.

Why do children like their parents? Because parents do not leave their children, no matter how bad they are, but rather try to pull them to a better place. They do not leave them as bad children. The desire of parents is more earnest than that of children in bad positions, which is why children like their parents. In this way, parents stand in a position of goodness before their children.

Similarly, when humans take after God's model and pursue God as the center of absolute goodness, and seek to manage everything and receive decisions from God, it is because God stands in the position of a parent. When humanity, the children of God, is sorrowful, God does not leave them alone; He digs into the valleys of sorrow and seeks to transform that sorrow into His own sorrow, standing in a position to grieve on their behalf. This is why we want to take Him as our model and completely become one with Him, wishing to live together with Him forever.

To become a model person, one must stand close to God
The closer one gets to God, the simpler the problems become. It is just God and me. However, when analyzing that simple content, it can represent the whole. This is because it can be the model of the universe and can deal with thousands and tens of thousands of people. Because there is content that can establish relationships in all directions based on goodness, the more one delves into it, the more infinite stimulation they can feel, and the more new aspects they can encounter. Humans can feel happiness there. The reason we pursue God is that He is such a God.

Today, scholars, literary figures, or global figures are those who, the closer they get to such vertical positions or to the center of human nature, can feel three-dimensional sensations. When they directly feel that sensation, they can express that content with certainty. What is expressed in this way cannot be anything other than a global literary work or a global theory.

Therefore, to stand in the true position of being a model, one must stand close to God. God is an eternal being and an infinite being, so He must possess infinite content along with His true nature. Therefore, it is not just about giving and ending; one must have a heart that can give a thousand or ten thousand times and still give more. This is what becomes the issue.

In your faith life, who can you take as a model on your journey to find God? It would be someone who can alleviate your sorrows when you are sorrowful. It would also be someone who can leave joy more eternally. Only then can they be a model. This is what God is like.

The joy felt centered on God is not temporary. It remains forever. The joy you felt in grace, whether through inspiration or revelation, or the joy you felt with those who believe in God is not temporary. It is something that will not be forgotten throughout your life. Why is that? Because it is close to the truth. The closer something is to the truth, the more eternal it is. The more it is in a position to be a model, the more it can establish relationships with the whole. Therefore, it cannot be forgotten.

In our faith life, our Unification Church members are in a position like a lamp. To be a central lamp in a dark world, the brightness of that lamp is what matters. It should not be a lamp that lights up temporarily and then goes out; it must be a being that can shine brighter and brighter as time goes on. To become such a being, one must establish a relative relationship centered on the model. Just as two can shine brighter when they establish a relationship and exchange with each other, the broader the connections that can be made, the more valuable light they can emit rather than diminishing.

In your faith life, God does not desire people who become lax or regress; He wishes for you to become people who can rise higher and higher. Therefore, you must be wide and high in your inner world of heart and in your external life, becoming a friend of God and a sanctuary where God can dwell. God will come to those who stand in such a true central position.

In your married life, if the husband is a model person in external aspects, he may seem happy externally. However, everything between husband and wife does not end in external aspects. While external conditions for happiness are of course necessary, he must also be able to provide the conditions for inner happiness to his wife. A husband like that cannot be a good husband. The wife also should not end as one who can only be praised in internal aspects. She must also be a wife who can be praised in external aspects. Both spouses must take positions where they can be models for each other.

Balance external and internal life well
Let’s think about what can be a model. External life is monotonous. After you have breakfast, you work, have lunch, work again, and then have dinner and sleep. It is monotonous like this. Then there is the task of raising children. This is also repetitive, so it is monotonous. However, it does not end as just monotonous. While human external life is monotonous, there is a side of internal life that is broad, high, and complex behind that external life. Only those who possess the inner capacity to freely move and push through all external monotonous environments will not fall into despair and hopelessness in those circumstances.

A couple who are happy just because they have established some foundation in their external life cannot be a model couple. Even if their external life is happy, to make that external life shine brighter and appear happier, they need to have broad and deep internal connections. This is necessary. Both the inside and outside must be equipped. One cannot have only one aspect. One cannot have only a flat aspect. One must have three-dimensional content. This is what becomes the issue.

When we look at our daily life, we are awake and active for more than twelve hours. If we sleep for about eight hours out of 24, what do we do with the remaining sixteen hours?
more than a mere external issue. If one lives solely focused on external problems, what will reinforce the internal? What will strengthen the internal connections that can drive external life forward? 

If a monotonous life becomes habitual and one thinks that is what human life is, then they are merely a person belonging to the world. One must develop that mundane living environment and create a life that imbues that environment with higher values. Only then can one determine a position of good in an evil world. A person who cannot lead a life that governs external living cannot be called a believer. They cannot be called a person of heaven.

Jesus’ external life was monotonous, but internally he lived for his nation and for all humanity. He possessed the value of such an internal life, felt it, and lived through that experience. Because Jesus lived such a broad, deep, and high internal life, he could become a friend of humanity in the historical age and inspire thousands of years of history to reflect his likeness.

It is important how I speak and what actions I take in my life. In a family, how does a mother treat her children, and how does a wife serve her husband? What kind of life is that? That life is a generalized life. You are all walking a generalized course. Is this good? Can it be good? Such human living cannot serve as a model. However, if it is something that is with God and is of greater value, then it can be said to be a model. Therefore, to live a life that is more valuable and can serve as a model, one must be close to God.

Become a model family before the world of Satan
How should a person on the side of heaven live? In a family, a wife should not treat her husband in a flat manner. She must treat him based on an internal life. Just because a husband treats his wife a bit differently than yesterday, the wife should not respond negatively. There should be no difference. If one treats the other well, they should feel a higher internal stimulus, and even if treated poorly, they should be able to supplement that negativity rather than criticize it. Such a wife is a necessary wife before her husband. Likewise, a husband must also be able to be that way before his wife for the family to progress.

However, a family that tears each other apart, finds faults, and harbors resentment will regress and be destroyed. In other words, they cannot avoid separation. You must understand this.

Thus, the standard that can serve as a model centered on the family is for the couple to acknowledge each other's value based on internal character and to support each other’s shortcomings. Only then can that family serve as a model in the external world of Satan.

A wife who treats her husband that way and a husband who treats his wife that way should not end there; as time goes on, they must expand their scope and make it three-dimensional. When they realize that the joys of their family are needed by all humanity, they must stand in a position to strive to proliferate and develop that joy before the world, becoming the center of goodness and a model of goodness representing God. You must understand this.

Let’s become models
What must we do to live such a life? We must connect our entire life with God. When something bad happens, do not try to resolve it among humans. Resolve it with God. Resolve it with faith. Also, when something good happens, do not center it around yourself. You must be able to rejoice with God. Although a relationship of give and take has begun between you and me, you must always think that the first connection and motivation is between God and you. A person who establishes a life system that relates all problems with God and seeks resolution with God will surely progress.

Let’s become people who evade Satan
In our lives, there is a time of indemnity. There are unhappy places in both normal and abnormal lives. However, we must not digest that unhappiness as unhappiness. When faced with an unhappy situation, do not try to resolve it alone; you must relate it to God and digest it.

So, what causes unhappiness in my life? It is because God is carrying out the history of indemnity. The history of indemnity involves nations and the world. In the history of indemnity, a good person must become a sacrifice; otherwise, indemnity cannot occur. That is the essence of restoration. Therefore, if a good person like myself stands in an unhappy place, I must understand that I am bearing a burden to save all people. Bearing such a burden is the rightful duty of love for God.

If there is a person who lives with God and digests life with God, everything they encounter begins with God and ends with God. Therefore, that person can give infinitely and still have more to give, becoming a subject capable of establishing infinite relationships. You must think about this.

Just because today is good, you should not say, “God, I am truly thankful for today.” Likewise, you should not say, “God, I was truly sad today,” just because you are sad. If it is good, be thankful for the good; if it is bad, be thankful for the bad. It may be a minus for me, but if it can be good for the public sphere, then I must be grateful for the whole. If my existence can make the whole good, then I must be grateful.

Thus, goodness is giving something good to the whole. Because goodness aims to give something more precious and broader, even if I am in a lonely and painful place, I must learn to be grateful. To give goodness to the world, I must also learn to be grateful for such pain.

As you know, Jeong Seok-on’s mother is Kim Seong-do, and both Kim Seong-do and Jeong Seok-on are people of gratitude. They are people who are thankful in every situation. Upon reflection, that is correct. A person who knows how to be grateful cannot be invaded by Satan. Even if Satan tries to invade, he will flee. Even if one is invaded by Satan, they must think, “God has given me trials to indemnify the whole.” When one encounters such a person once, twice, three times... the more they encounter them, the more they will find themselves failing, so Satan will not approach them even if invited. However, the more one tries to evade this, the more Satan will follow them.

God should originally be a God who only deals with good things, but due to the fall of humanity, He has been forced into a sorrowful position. Therefore, God could not help but take on all that sorrow to unite with these humans. Without a sorrowful expression, without standing in a position that is not sorrowful, He cannot be a good God, a God of joy. He cannot be a God who can have a starting point of joy.

Thus, God has walked a laborious path for this sorrowful earth until now. If He had thought that the path was too difficult and painful to walk, goodness would not have been able to start. However, no matter how hard and difficult it was, He walked this path because it was the way to goodness and the way to find the shining value of goodness. Even if this path leads to death, He sought infinite happiness and eternal joy along the way.

Although the start was not a joyful one, without a God who could wrap sorrowful content in joy and digest it into joy, a joyful heaven could not be achieved.

Therefore, Jesus did not pray for his own joy or happiness. When praying in the Garden of Gethsemane, he said, “Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not my will, but yours be done.” What is the Father’s will? It is to take on the sorrows of all people. It is to take on the deaths and sufferings of all people. Even if Jesus is sacrificed, the Father’s will is to present happiness to all people.

In the face of such a Father’s will, when one is infinitely pained, infinitely fearful, and confronted with the final barrier, it may be despairing, but one must not despair at that moment; rather, they must transcend that despair and hold onto hope. Jesus crossed that peak with the belief that the path he was taking was not a path of ruin but a path for a new beginning, and from there, a new history of joyful Christianity began.

Let’s absorb the bad and transform it into elements of life
If more than two-thirds of your life consists of unspeakable misery and pain, can you just throw away that two-thirds of your life? No, you cannot. You cannot throw it away. It will always follow you.

We are fallen descendants, born as a result of the consequences of sin from our ancestors. Therefore, there are highs and lows in our lives. Can we then discard the lows and only take the highs? No, we cannot. We must accept everything as our fate, and if there is joy in the high, we must lift the sorrow that has fallen into despair based on that joy. We must possess the capacity for joy and hope. From that standpoint, we must engage in our faith life, which is the path of life for fallen humanity today.

Here, what you must understand is that when you say, “I must establish a model of love. I must establish a model of life. I must establish a model of life. I must establish a model of character. I must establish a model of my family. Or I must establish a model in society and the nation,” it does not only contain good things; rather, there are more bad things than good. More than two-thirds are bad. Good things do not appear. Even in the social pages of newspapers, there are more bad articles than good ones. Almost all articles are negative.

For this reason, those who wish to digest this world and create a good world are being pushed around by these things and chased by them. However, we must swallow this and digest it to make it a source of nourishment. We must calmly plant the internal goodness of God and use the elements of evil as fertilizer or nutrients to develop. Only then can we have vitality.

The dirty things are bad, but when they are absorbed as fertilizer for life to grow, even that dirt becomes necessary. When seeds are sown in a place where dirty fertilizer is spread, it does not matter to the seeds. Even if the seeds are in ashes or manure, when they take root and absorb it to gain vitality, that fertilizer becomes a factor for the growth of living things. Likewise, even if you face trials and pains, if you possess the subjective ability to digest those trials and pains, you can become a shining being throughout eternity.

Today, our Unification Church is also on a path toward the evil world. Along that path, there is happiness in the Unification Church and a standard of goodness, but that happiness and standard of goodness do not appear first. They must first walk the path of indemnity and the path of responsibility and mission, which is why they appear first as evil and sorrowful. If they appeared only as good, anyone could walk that path. That is why they manifest as sorrowful.

That sorrow is a sorrow of the denomination, but it is also a sorrow that can represent the nation and the world. The greater, higher, and broader that sorrow is, the more it is an indemnity to globalize the Unification Church. It does not destroy the Unification Church. Thus, when one possesses the subjective ability to digest everything and crosses the peak, the Unification Church can lay a global foundation.

The Unification Church must become a model for the world
Why do I always urge you to overcome? Because there is hope in enduring and overcoming. However, overcoming does not mean crying and struggling while getting through. True overcoming means getting through even if it is difficult, but doing so in a way that does not appear difficult. Even if it is sad, one must get through without showing sadness. That is true overcoming. It is not grudgingly getting through; it is enduring and getting through. Even if it is lonely, sad, and painful, one must be able to digest it with joy and get through it; only then can one transform the evil and hell into heaven. That is how one can serve as a true believer and become a foundation for personal models in the world. Furthermore, it will become a foundation for collective models, and you must understand this.

If you live for 70 to 80 years and two-thirds of that time is a sad life, what should you do with that two-thirds? You must create a joyful life centered on God. You must transform it into a heavenly life. Heaven is a place where one lives by giving. God must also give. Parents must give to their children. Even after giving good things, if there are even better things, parents want to give those as well. Isn’t that true? No matter how much you dress your children in nice clothes or feed them good food, they are not satisfied with that; they want to do even better for them. Wanting to give better things after giving is the heart of parents and the heart of God. Therefore, when two-thirds of your life is said to be unhappy, the question is how you will digest that. Everyone has peaks in their lives. It is important whether you have the qualifications to break down those peaks and digest them.

If God were to give you a reward, where would that reward be given? Would it be given in a place where all people can see? No, it can certainly be given there, but it can also be given in the opposite place. Rather than in a place where many people follow because they think it is good, it is given in the final place. If God has one treasure, He wants to give it only to one person. He dislikes it when everyone follows. He wants to give it to those who survive, to those who have survived the brink of death.

So, where will you receive this reward? You must decide this issue. Even if pain comes to you, you must not despair. Some will receive rewards in joyful places, and some will receive rewards in sorrowful places. Some will feel joy and receive grace, while others will receive grace through entering sorrow. That cannot be avoided. Because the relationships of hierarchy and the relationships of front, back, left, and right are intertwined, not everyone is the same.

When reading a certain book, one person may be infinitely impressed and recognize it as having absolute value, while another may think, “What’s so special about it?” and feel no emotion at all. Why is that? It is because the direction of perception is different. Because the situation of reading is different, that book does not have the same impact on everyone.
Even if it is good, it does not bring about an emotional response. Some people can approach God in a joyful place, while others can approach God in a sorrowful place. Therefore, grace comes in various forms. There are different types of the Holy Spirit, such as the Holy Spirit like fire, like water, like clouds, and like silk, right? They are all different. One might think, "Why is it that while person A lives happily, I am suffering like this?" However, suffering does not necessarily mean unhappiness. In fact, one can be much happier despite suffering. It is possible to be better than anyone else. That is the potential we have.

Currently, our Unification Church is walking the path of suffering and pain, but this is not an unhappy situation. In fact, it is happier than the established churches. We are ahead of them by a step. Therefore, we can be a model in this wicked world or in the future world. We can also be revered by all.

If one feels happiness even amidst suffering, that person is the happiest. This does not mean they are suffering. Those who enjoy happiness easily fall into despair when they enter a place of suffering, but those who go down to find happiness cannot easily fall. For such people, happiness continues to come as time goes on. Understanding this, you should lead a difficult life. Even in the midst of hardship, you should be able to say, "Oh, how wonderful." Satan always seeks to enter a good place, so goodness is fleeting. Therefore, the ability to digest difficult and sorrowful situations is what constitutes a graceful and healthy life of faith.

The purpose of indemnity is to move to a position of grace. Thus, even when faced with sorrowful events, we should understand that it is natural to digest that sorrow with joy alongside God. If we think of walking the path of indemnity for the nation and the world, we will find joy regardless of the difficulties we face. If we consider it a position of grace given by God for the world's indemnity, even if that person is not directly related to the world, they enter a position of national and global value. By shedding tears and praying for the nation and the world, and overcoming hardships silently with gratitude, one enters a position of national and global value.

One must become a person who can claim grace even without being given grace. If grace is given to help one do well, but they fail to do so, they lose grace instead. However, if a person who has not received grace digests their situation as if they have received grace, dedicating their life for the world and being grateful before God, then grace will be transferred to that person. In this sense, it is said, "Those who seek to live will die, and those who seek to die will live."

A place where one takes from others is not a place of laughter and dancing. A place where one receives more valuable content is not a place for joy but a place of tension. A place of tension is where sorrow and pain intersect. It is a place that binds and releases everything.

Where did Jesus go after he died? It was unjust to die on the cross on this earth, but where did he go for three days after his death? He went to hell. That was a test. For humanity, death is the greatest fear, but for Jesus, going to hell was the ultimate object of fear. So, did Jesus become the master of fear in hell, or the master of happiness? You must understand that during those three days in hell, Jesus was concerned with becoming someone who could overcome the pains of hell.

From this perspective, believers should not flow along with the wickedness of this world or the sorrow of this world. Rather, they should block that wickedness and sorrow and present conditions for joy. Because wicked people need us, if we become central figures in that environment, we can become models.

In that sense, God is the central being that serves as a model for the universe. This is because God does not look upon the suffering of all people with despair and lamentation but is the one who can overcome all suffering and appear as the master of new hope, thus becoming a model for humanity. You must understand this.

Let us emulate God. In your life of faith, you will have to give up the best for yourself. However, just because you lose the best does not mean you are unhappy. If God needs an offering, you must give the best, right? Therefore, losing the best means you are being taken for an offering. Why is this taken? Because you do not know how to offer, God may take it instead.

If you think this way, you will not end your difficulties with difficulty but will be able to welcome those difficulties with joy, and that joy will remain as a solid foundation before God. You must understand that difficult moments will come to see the beginning of that joy.

When speaking, one must bind and move on. What must be bound? That binding is difficult. To bind, this point must go to that point, and that point must come to this point. It must be reversed. Only then can it be bound. Is that not so? It is the same. What seems bad can bear good fruit. It is a replacement. It is a reversal. Satan goes to God's side, and God goes to Satan's side. It is a switch. Therefore, binding is not an easy task. However, to reverse, it cannot be done.

There are times in your life when binding occurs. You will draw some archetype. You bind through several generations, dozens, hundreds, or thousands. If your ancestors were evil, the knots will be many. The knots will be small and numerous. However, if your ancestors were good, the knots will be large and not many. Those knots are not for oneself but are sacrificial knots for the nation and the state. And we must become that way.

So where is heaven? Heaven is said to be in your heart. It is not easy for heaven to enter my heart. Heaven can only enter my heart after overcoming the adversities of life and the world of Satan. That is why the history of indemnity unfolds to break down the world of Satan.

You must digest sorrow into joy as you move forward centered on your purpose. Just as God became a model for all people, we too must digest sorrow and evil to become manifestations of joy and glory. Also, since God overcame the path of suffering to appear before us, we too must take God as our model and stand in the same position to live our lives of faith. By doing so, you must understand that you can become the sons and daughters of God by testifying in the world.

<Words> The path we Unification Church members walk is not a personal path. While the providence of restoration is governed by God alone, it is a historical purpose.

We know that the historical process has a past, a present, and a future. Therefore, you must understand that the path we walk must be the path that should have been in the past, the path that should be in the present, and the path that should be in the future. That path is not different from the past, nor is it different from the present, nor is it different from the future. The past is that path, the present is that path, and the future is that path.

We must traverse that path.

From this perspective, the question arises as to whether the path we walk can indeed replace the past, present, and future. In other words, the journey from the moment we are born as a life on this earth until we reach the spirit world must be a path that can replace history, replace the era, and replace the future.

The Mission of Humanity Viewed from the Origin of Existence
Thus, even though I, as an individual living in the weight of history, may be small, I do not end as just an individual.

Originally, we humans were not born of our own volition. Nor were we born under the plan of our parents to have such and such sons and daughters. We are not born according to the demands of our parents.

When we delve into the origins of our existence centered on God's providence, we must conclude that we humans were sent to this earth as living beings to fulfill a significant responsibility in relation to the origin of that providence and the history that moves around that origin.

When we think about the fact that we humans were born in relation to God's providential will and God's historical plan, we must not remain as we are in reality. If you are a young person in your twenties, you should not just remain as a young person in your twenties. We must feel that we are indeed entities that can define this history and replace this providence.

That "I," in other words, the "I" who is aware of history and aware of heavenly principles, the "I" who knows heaven and history centered on heaven, and not only knows but can also take responsibility for heaven and history, is what countless prophets and sages have longed for. The path that all who have come and gone in the historical age have sought is to establish an "I" that can replace history and providence, fulfilling the mission before history and the mission before providence, and pursuing a victorious appearance.

If the people of the Republic of Korea are descendants of Dangun, they will all come forth following their grandfather Dangun. Not only that, but we are also connected to God, who is the origin of all existence.

God is manifest on this earth, and the world’s humanity is manifest, and countless prophets and sages who have come and gone in the past are manifest, and our ancestors are manifest, and our nation is manifest. This means that fallen humanity carries a destiny to transcend this history and era. And those who can transcend that destiny are those who are close to the end, and the closer they are to the end, the greater their responsibility.

My Position to Achieve the Final Victory
So, what kind of person is a group or individual that can determine the final victory? There must be a specific nation, but before there is a specific nation, there must be a specific tribe. And before there is a specific tribe, there must be a specific family, and before there is a specific family, there must be a specific individual. This is the position of such an individual. Therefore, it is essential to recognize that I am not just "I" who is dependent on the world, but "I" who can embrace the world.

From the perspective of this historical providence and the historical process, the ultimate purpose of providential history can only be concluded by us in the present, not by God, nor by past people. Whether it is a tribe, a nation, a state, or the world, it will be opened by someone who represents heaven and earth.

This is the position of the individual today that you must understand.

From this conscious position, when I stand in this era, it may outwardly seem like a position that represents humanity, represents all environments, and represents heaven, appearing to be a very peaceful, happy, and hopeful position, but in reality, it cannot help but be an extremely lonely, sorrowful, and burdensome position. You must recognize that this is the current situation.

Why is that? Because the world has not yet become a place where I can take such a free environment with my heart, and because, centered on God's will, the world has not yet become a place where His will can be fulfilled, and because the foundation of hope that humanity can aspire to cannot be established in the natural environment we possess.

When I stand in such a position, bearing the responsibility to lead my family, my nation, and the world, it cannot be a trivial matter. I am the one who can represent history, I am the one who can represent the era, and I am the one who must prepare the origin of the future. Therefore, even though my life may only be that of an individual, the feelings, emotions, and all the connections of the living environment that person experiences are not limited to the individual but can represent the whole.

I must become one with the providence.
Then how should that position be? It must be formal. It must be an official position. A formal position is not something that can be altered by A and B. When you solve a math problem, you do it through formulas. The past was solved through those formulas, and even after a thousand years, it must be solved through those formulas. There is no objection to this.

Therefore, just because I can do as I please and say, "I went this way," does not guarantee that it is a formula. Doing as one pleases does not hold. The value of the formula is only revealed from the standpoint of the results that come from it. The problem lies here.

Then, what is the formula that humanity seeks to find in the historical age, a formula that can represent history, a formula that can find the heavenly principle, or a formula that can center around the whole issue and can be the first origin or starting factor? Today, we speak of "intention." Intention is relative. It exists because I exist. Intention can be said to be the will to pursue a purpose. From that standpoint, the problem is "I."

Therefore, even if there is a formula, it must become one with me, and I must harmonize with that formula and become a representation of that formula. Otherwise, it cannot be a formula. Thus, each of you must become such a self.

From this perspective, today, an official existence that can represent history, an official existence that can represent the era, an official existence that can represent the future, does not exist separately from the three eras. The formula is one. Who is that one? It is myself.

Therefore, when I stand in that position, "History is for the purpose of being in harmony with me." Why? Because it is a formula. And "This era is also for the purpose of being in harmony with me. The future cannot start without me." Why? Because it is a formula.

Then what is the essence that can become a formula? It is not something that can be expressed in numerical terms. I must become myself, transcending the numerical content. Then who can be that historical, official existence, that era-centered official existence, that future-centered official existence? Everything starts from there, and it passes through that, and everything resembles it, so this becomes the center.

An official central existence rooted in love
Today, every religion speaks of the concept of the Messiah. There must be a central existence referred to as the Savior or Redeemer. If that central existence is based on some specific religion, then it is not an official existence. A representative limited to a century or an era cannot be an official existence. Nor can a representative who can replace the historical era of Asia in any future historical process be an official existence. If this can be altered by anyone, if it can be moved at will by humans, then a future world cannot be established. This formula cannot be moved by individuals. History cannot move it either. The present world cannot move it, nor can the future. Moreover, it must become an unmovable center. Because everything must be connected through this center, the world today seeks this central existence. They wish for it based on their own lives, their own purposes, and claim it as today's religion. Among religions, it is Christianity.

When we speak of the official center itself, where is its root? It is rooted in love. Then what kind of love is that? It is not the love between a man and a woman that you speak of. It is God's love. It is rooted in God's love. It is not a love that can connect the love between you and me. Because it is connected to God's love, that connection has a historical love connection. It has become a connection based on that foundation.

Therefore, that love is not centered on me alone. It has replaced history and is a love that has established a relationship with the era. It is God's love that serves as the standard for the beginning that will continue eternally into the future.

Then what kind of path is ours? We must express the historical love of God through an official path, reveal the era's love of God, and act as the starting point for future love. Standing in such a position, we must be an official being that can replace the historical era and stand before the heavenly principle without shame. We must become such an existence. Then what kind of position is that? It is a position that has a connection between the absolute being and the relative being.

The highest purpose that humanity seeks
What is the highest purpose that humans seek? It may be to create and embrace one world. However, this is ultimately a relative purpose. No matter how much one embraces this world, a person who does not have a foundation of emotional awareness within it is unhappy.

For example, let’s say a person from South Korea has achieved independence for the world, overcoming all difficulties and bringing the world into a glorious state, fulfilling the desires of the heavenly principle. Let’s say they celebrate that joyful day. However, at that moment of joy, if they lose the person they love most dearly on this earth, that is, if they confront the moment of losing the absolute object of love that their individual self demands at the moment they can rejoice in finding the world, what will happen to them?

When considering that position, would they say, "I wanted to control this world as I please, and now that the moment of my purpose has come, I only need this moment, and I do not need my loved one"? Would they say, "This is all I need"? That is not the issue. If there is a way to prevent the death of their loved one, they would want to sacrifice that day of finding the world to save their loved one. From this perspective, it is not the relative world that is the issue, but the love that can become the foundation of internal emotional awareness.

You can feel this in your daily life. If someone has wealth and treasures that they can boast about in the world, and if their parents were to pass away, if that person emphasizes their love for their parents and values it, they would invest all their wealth, which they consider precious, if there were a way for their parents to live. Would they not be able to abandon everything external that they consider precious? Likewise, a parent who loves their child would want to save their child, even if it means sacrificing their own life, if that child were to face such a fate.

Considering all these issues, the official origin centered on oneself is God's love. It has been said that the relationship between God and humanity is that of a parent and child, and this relationship is irreplaceable. It does not require bargaining. It transcends human conditions and cannot be debated. It transcends the relative distance between you and me. God demands this position of love.

Therefore, we must walk with God, who has come through the historical era. We must discover the relationship of parent and child along the path we are taking. I must explore the emotional world reflected in God's providence of restoration over 6,000 years. From the family of Adam through Noah, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus, countless prophets and saints have sacrificed throughout the 2,000 years of Christian history since Jesus. I must not be ignorant of the world of God's sorrowful heart that has been traced through that burden.

The great realization of Jesus

The Essence of Love
You must understand that the significance of the cross exists because Jesus Christ died in this way. Jesus went to God even in death because He knew God's will. We must not complain. We must not make excuses. We cannot make excuses. Why is parental love precious? What does this mean? Vertical love must inevitably create horizontal love. Parental love is formed based on this principle, centered on God's love, and is realized in both vertical and horizontal dimensions. This is why parental love, which bears the elements of both dimensions, wants to give its precious things to its children just as they are. It allows them to receive as they are and seeks to expand horizontally. The essence of love is like that. 

Why is the essence of love like this? It is because love occurs in a relative relationship. The relationship between the subject and the object cannot be otherwise. The subject and the object create a circle through giving and receiving. The subject is vertical, and the object is horizontal, thus forming a circle at a 90-degree angle. Therefore, the essence of love must contain both vertical and horizontal elements. Among these, which comes first? The vertical comes first. That is why love flows from parents. When analyzing the inner heart of love, there is the essence of both vertical and horizontal love.

The Fundamental Teachings of the Unification Church

The Correct Parent-Child Relationship
Your families must establish an inseparable relationship centered on father and mother, both externally and internally. The success or failure of that family can be seen in how the parents and children relate to each other. That is, when parents love their children, do they love them for the sake of the children, or do they love them for their own sake? And when children honor their parents, do they follow and respect them for their own sake, or do they love and respect their parents beyond themselves? These are the issues.

Thus, when we speak of loving parents and loving children, those who love their parents centered on themselves cannot become true filial children. If parents love their children to fulfill their own interests and desires, then that love cannot be true parental love. In other words, if love is centered on oneself and is done because one needs it, then the love parents have for their children and the love children have for their parents cannot be true love.

A person does not exist solely for themselves. Parents exist for their children, and children also exist for their parents. If a relationship of parent and child is established based on the path of love, then that family cannot be broken by anyone. If someone tries to break that family, they will defend it even at the cost of their lives.

However, if there is a family where parents need their children and love them based on themselves, and children need their parents and love them based on themselves, then that family can be broken. If such a family faces increasing threats or dire situations that threaten their lives, the parents and children of that family will become divided.

However, if children love their parents and parents love their children beyond themselves, then the bond of parent and child will be firmly established, and if they feel each other's value and live together, no one can separate them. Not even with a knife or any threat can they be divided. No power of any nation can sever that bond. Even if there is fear and threat that takes lives, that love cannot be conquered.

Everyone seeks such love, such a family. If there is a family that does not have such love, they want to emulate a family that does have such love. This is the original intention of humanity that you all know well. If you educate your children, you would want them to take the children of such families as examples, and if your parents are not such parents, you would want them to become like those parents.

If there is a family centered on such a relationship of parent and child, no law or social system can break or separate that relationship. There may be laws to firmly establish and thoroughly protect the relationship of parent and child in that family, but there cannot be laws that weaken or separate it. If such a relationship of parent and child is severed, that family will collapse, society will collapse, and a true nation cannot be formed. At the same time, a true world cannot be formed either.
