Can you split the world from such a position?

For this reason, the Teacher makes you suffer to the point of death. You may have thought you would hear good words when you meet the Teacher today, but the Teacher's gift is to tell you to suffer to the point of death. (Laughter) Suffer to the point of death. What should you suffer for? "For the world." Not for Teacher Moon, not for the Unification Church. You must suffer for the world. That world will come in the future. It will come holding the flag of liberation. When you die, there will come a day when millions will erect a tombstone in front of your grave and praise you. It is because I know this that I do these things.

After passing this path, your life will be remembered as a precious life for thousands and tens of thousands of years. The torn undershirt and worn-out dress shirt you wore while living like that will be regarded by your descendants as treasures that cannot be bought even for a thousand pieces of gold. Do you understand that? The Teacher has collected all the torn shirts and pants he wore during three years of suffering in Hungnam Prison. They have become like treasures due to ammonia and acid. However, he saved them for three years to leave them behind. If the path the Teacher walks is not wrong, the opposing nations and the world will not be able to establish their opposing intentions and will ultimately be pushed out by the Teacher. At that time, what has been saved will become a treasure that descendants can hold onto and cry out for thousands of years. It is precious because it becomes the material that can silently shape history. How much is the undershirt the Teacher wore worth? It is worth less than a penny, but the blood and sweat shed for the world while wearing it cannot be exchanged for thousands of pieces of gold.

**The Question of Whom You Live For**
Jesus was born as the son of a carpenter and was a friend of fishermen by the Sea of Galilee. But that is not the issue. The question is, for whom did he die? For whom did he shed blood and sweat, and for whom did he live? In that era, Nazareth Jesus was condemned as a traitor to the nation, a destroyer of society, and an instigator, yet who would have thought that he would establish the Christian cultural sphere of the world today and create a new world connection?

God is alive. God will surely save this world and lead it to a new world. That is why He has brought this world to the end times. At this point, we Unification Church members must have a deeper heart and become the sons and daughters that God longs for. We must become sons and daughters who embrace and love the world. God wants to love such sons and daughters. Furthermore, God has gone through various humiliations and historical hardships to establish such families. Is this not the path of restoration sought for 6,000 years?

If the Unification Church attempts to horizontally indemnify this vertical history, we cannot refuse any trials or pains that come our way, even if they are a millennium of resentment. Even if we die, we must die saying we die for the world and plant the flag of victory. Then, because of that flag, we will be able to praise that nation with a value beyond thousands of pieces of gold, and when the sovereignty of that nation is restored, we will be placed among the ranks of loyal subjects and surely be established in the heavenly world as the center of heaven. When we think of these facts, is this not the greatest hope that humanity should pursue?

Even if the bedding of a person living for the world looks like a miserable rag that is worth less than a single won, a rag that even beggars would not take, there will come a time when this will change, and they will be able to live under a golden blanket. (The recording pauses momentarily)

**Love God and Humanity Even in Difficult Situations**
What kind of educational background did Mary have? Did Mary graduate from college or high school? Mary must have been an uneducated woman. Why? Because in the five books of Moses, a virgin who becomes pregnant is to be stoned to death. Yet, when the angel Gabriel appeared and told her that she would conceive and bear a son, she said, "I do not know a man; how can this happen?" However, when the angel said that with God nothing is impossible, she replied, "Let it be to me according to your word." Mary, who so simply accepted such an enormous issue, must have been an uneducated woman.

However, Mary represented the women of Israel with her heart, cared for Israel, and with the privilege of being the chosen people of Israel, she loved the world more than anyone else and earnestly prayed to love God, hoping to connect with Him. She was a woman who prayed a lot. When we think about this, it shows that knowledge or appearance is not the issue.

The Teacher did not buy his own clothes until he was 30 years old. It was not because he had no money or no food. So, in terms of external appearances, you may seem more excellent than me. But why was that? Because I have children whom I govern and care for, but I have not been able to do anything for them with all my heart. Only after I have given my heart and love to my children do I want to wear clothes myself. This is the teaching of virtue and the heart of a parent. Because I could not establish such a position, I could not buy my own clothes.

Also, the Teacher has never had a day without hunger in his 30 years of life. It is not because there was no money in our house. There was money, but that money was not spent for the Teacher. If someone was lying sick in the street and could not go home, he would pour all his strength into carrying them over a thousand miles to help them. He has done such things.

The Teacher has not avoided any tasks. He has done all kinds of things beyond the potato rock of Gangwon-do. He has experienced everything that a human can do. He has accepted everything without avoiding any task. Even when going to prison and being tortured, he did not go out as a coward. He became a man who met God in an environment where he could taste life and judge life. He has been moved by God and has come this far. Even if 30 million people oppose him and insult him for 100 or 300 years, let them do it.

You must understand that even if you live in a valley in Gangwon-do, you can live for the world. Unification Church members must love the world more than their husbands and love God more than anyone else. Do you understand? "Yes." Then, is that a loss? It is not a loss; it is a blessing. Look, when you love God, does God's love come to you or not? And when you love the world, will all the people of the world support you or not?

**Become Someone You Can Be Proud of Before All People**
Do you want to be able to boast about yourself before everyone, or not? To boast, you must have something to boast about; can you boast about having nothing? If you can boast, you should be able to say, "I can receive God's love. I can receive the support of all people." Would it be good or bad to be a husband or wife who can receive love? If you can live with such love, where when I go, they follow, and when I stay, they can stay, you will not perish.

Do you like Teacher Moon of the Unification Church? "Yes." Why do you like him? Because you love him so much, the Teacher is being insulted. There are many people who cannot distinguish whether it is day or night. In the early morning while the Teacher is sleeping, they come over the wall and ask, "Is the Teacher here?" Women crawl over the wall looking for the Teacher. So, it is inevitable that he gets insulted. Did the Teacher call for them? At that time, the Teacher scolds them thoroughly. However, the Teacher does not feel guilty. No matter what the world says, he does not feel guilty. Even when dragged to prison and mocked, the Teacher does not feel guilty. He is dignified.

When the Teacher entered the Seodaemun Prison, as soon as he stepped through the door, the warden glared and said, "So, the leader of the Unification Church, Moon, has come." He spoke as if mocking. At that moment, the Teacher thought, "Let’s see if you surrender to me or not." He believed the rumors were true and treated the Teacher that way. Gradually, he realized that Teacher Moon was not that kind of person, and later he even wanted to talk to the Teacher, offering his lunch box. That person will have a chance to meet the Teacher someday.

At that time, he heard all sorts of things. "What are you, and what are you doing...?" The Teacher thought, "Well, you guys, do whatever you want. I will accept it all." Then, within less than a month, the Teacher had made them like his servants. At that time, it was an emergency operation. "You little brat, aren't you this kind of brat?" And when the Teacher came out after three months, the warden, the section chief, and the pastors of established churches there all came to the Unification Church. Do you know that? They realized that the rumors were different.

Unification Church ladies, that is why the Unification Church members follow the Teacher day and night. Even if they get insulted, they are okay with it. (Laughter) The prison staff were surprised to see those ladies. Later, quite a problem arose. From early morning, they would fight to see the Teacher. Even if it was their own children, if there were rumors, they would all hush up. It was okay for a day or two, but as the Teacher's release approached, it became more and more intense, and they wondered why. The Teacher evangelized the prison warden.

When the Teacher kept quiet, angels appeared in the spirit world and told them, "You go and greet Moon! And when he comes in, offer everything." How wonderful is that? This is how the invisible spirit world operates. So, whose side are you on? "God's side." Is it God's side? It is my side. (Laughter) The Teacher lives on in such a way, even if he is lonely.

**The Unification Church Has Grown into a Global Church**
When the Teacher entered the communist world in the North, over 80 established church pastors signed a petition to kill Teacher Moon. After that, they sat there saying it would be refreshing now that Teacher Moon was going to die, but why would the Teacher die? In the end, all those who conspired to kill the Teacher ended up dead. The communists killed them all. The ones who had imprisoned him to kill him came out alive, while those who wanted to kill him died. Is this a good thing or a bad thing? "It is good."
"That's a good thing, isn't it? But you shouldn't hope for that for yourselves. The teacher has been to prison in the communist world, so he knows a lot about it. During the Japanese occupation, the teacher was involved in underground movements in Tokyo with communists during the day. At that time, he realized that in the future, he would become enemies with them. It's truly a sorrowful thing. I know that this is also our pain. The teacher knew well that communists would become enemies, but before that, Japan was our enemy, which is why he did all sorts of things with the communists. He came out like this to save the country. The teacher thought as he left Japan, 'I will surely return in 20 years, so let's meet again then. Right now, I cannot repay the emperor of Japan, and I cannot resolve the grief of our nation, but in the future, there will come a time when I will command and teach the people of your country, your youth. Let's meet again then.' He had such thoughts.

After that, the teacher went back to Japan after 20 years. As soon as he arrived, what he was most curious about was how many young men and women there were in our church. About 500 young men and women gathered, and they were all children of wealthy families. He told them that Japan is our enemy, but he had sent them special envoys and provided them with resources to save them. He asked the young people gathered there if they knew what their country's sin was, and they said they did. Then he asked if they knew what the Unification Church was, and they said they did. He then asked what they should do in the future, and they all said they would do whatever the teacher said. How wonderful is this? They said they didn't need the emperor of Japan, and they hoped for the victory of the Unification Church and its founder. When the teacher commands them, they said they would do anything. This is the Unification Church.

Right now, the World Anti-Communist League (WACL) conference is probably in full swing in Japan. It must have started at 1:30 PM today. A senator from the United States is supposed to give a congratulatory speech there. Do you know who arranged that? The highest leader who is manipulating it from behind is here. (Laughter) There are members of the Japanese Liberal Democratic Party and former prime ministers who have been caught up in my operation, dancing and enjoying themselves. First of all, they are excited.

I have received insults from this nation, and although rumors have spread, what wrong have I done to the Republic of Korea? If Japan becomes a pro-communist country, there will be no way for the Republic of Korea to survive. That is why I have been planning for the past ten years and have been fighting with tears of blood until now. In this era where our nation cannot find its place, where is the turning point, and who should play the role of a guide? We must do that.

Now, even the intelligence agencies and others are all approving us. If it weren't for us, they wouldn't be able to instill anti-communist ideology in the future. Do you know that, or not? "We know." However, the anti-communist alliance talks about how the founder of the Unification Church has no name and so on. That's right. The teacher is not a well-known founder. But he is not unqualified. The teacher thinks so. Is he qualified or not? "He is." Just wait and see. They will fall into the teacher's operation.

You may not know what kind of battles we fought in April, May, and June. You don't know, but we fought incredible battles. Someone related to the intelligence agency may be here, but listen. They say that the scale of the Unification Church is so large that it doesn't fit their compass. Their compass is too small to grasp where our end reaches. The Republic of Korea is currently in a situation where it is struggling to survive, yet we are trying to solve the Asian problem centered on the world and talking about the Japanese issue. Are we doing that? Are we great people or foolish people?

We are great, and we have been inspired. Not with a bad wind, but with a good wind that carries the fragrance of flowers on a spring day. It is different from the autumn wind. The founder of the Unification Church is always in spring. He always feels good. No matter how much opposition there is, he feels good. Even if there are unpleasant things, he feels good. He lets go of bad things. Just wait and see. When I hold a feast later, those who opposed me will not be able to say a word even if I don't give them a piece of rice cake.

So when I bless 700 couples, I plan to hold a feast. Since the population of Seoul is about 5 million, I will make 5 million rice cakes. So the teacher wants to distribute them all. Let's make 5 million rice cakes. Would it be good to make them or not? "It would be good." Then how many should be made in Gangwon Province? Since the country has 8 provinces, how many should be made in Gangwon Province? If we divide 5 million by 8, how much is that? About 600,000, right? Therefore, we need to make 600,000. 600,000 would probably fill a truck. Will you make 600,000 or not?

The conclusion is to love God and the world to the utmost.
God has graciously taught you the condition of indemnity. If we set the condition to make 60 rice cakes instead of 600,000, it will all end there. (Laughter) Unification Church members set conditions on top of what the teacher has already done, no matter how global the task is. The teacher takes all the beatings of the world first. Isn't that right?

Will you buy six rice cakes with God's heart or not? "I will." Will one person buy six, or will the whole group buy six? "Just one." Then buy and bring them out. (Laughter) You may not have bought six rice cakes, but did you prepare them? "Yes." Everyone, are you feeling good this morning? "Yes." The teacher is also feeling excited. (Laughter) Just wait and see. At this feast, people from all over the world will gather.

I directed the operations of the WACL conference currently being held in Japan. If the president of the association doesn't know anything, he should follow what the teacher says, and it will be fun and work well. Do you know such things? "Yes." Because of such things, Unification Church members listen only to the words of the teacher of the Unification Church rather than their parents. Isn't that right? "Yes." Whether they hear it at night, during the day, or in the evening, they are grateful. There is nothing more unpleasant than not listening to words. Originally, you are supposed to listen well, right? "Yes." Our young ladies, is that right? "Yes." What about the older ladies? "Yes." That's how it is.

In the end, what are we trying to do? We are trying to love the world once. We want to live for the world and love it madly, and live for God and be mad about God's love. Even if we have to sacrifice our grown sons and daughters to offer sacrifices, we want to go crazy for once. If we fail, then they can cut off the teacher's neck.

Even now, there are many people who would stab the teacher in the neck in broad daylight. However, they will not be able to stab me. They will perish first. Do you understand?

Our Unification Church may be dying, but it is rising. We are going the opposite way. When I think of this, the path for Unification Church members is nothing but a path of hardship.

When I look at you, I see that you have nothing. There may not be much money in the teacher's wallet either. When the teacher came here this morning, he asked his mother for some money to bring with him. Because if someone comes from far away without travel expenses, the teacher has to provide for them.

Be a messenger of love.
We must become a delivering nation. What does delivery mean? A delivering nation is a nation of messengers. (Laughter) Isn't that right? When waiting for a loved one who has gone far away, whose news comes? "The messenger." It comes by letter, right? That letter comes through the messenger. Isn't that right? "Yes." When you receive that letter, is it good or bad? "It's good."

But has anyone among you ever treated a messenger well? While waiting for a letter with eager eyes, when the messenger delivers the letter, there are people who happily receive it and run into their rooms, but no one treats the messenger to lunch and says, 'Please eat before you go.' The messenger is pitiful. He delivers kind news to countless people, but is there anyone who pays taxes to the messenger after receiving their salary? If there is even one lady who has treated a messenger politely, please raise your hand. It is said that no one has ever treated a pitiful person.

I have asked Unification Church members to take on the mission of the messenger, but have they become messengers who bring good news to every household? Is there a messenger who, while delivering a letter, says, 'Today the weather is really nice. Why am I sweating so much?' and asks the owner for a cool glass of water while climbing up to the porch? The messenger is treated poorly. Isn't that right?

A delivering nation is a nation of messengers. This is said regarding our Unification Church. We must become messengers of love. We want to be a nation of messengers who deliver God's love to the world. How wonderful is this? What kind of nation? A delivering nation.

What does the term 'white-clad nation' mean? When burying the dead, do we not wear white clothes? (Laughter) White clothes are used as a marker. What are white clothes for? They are used as a marker. In the pitch-black night, can something red or yellow serve as a marker? Only white can serve as a marker. In the dark world filled with death, only white, centered on God's love, can serve as a marker. The teacher can say that he has carried out this work centered on Unification Church teachings.

The true path of love that must be followed even in death.
The teacher has walked a lonely path until now. Even now, he is lonely. It is not because he cannot meet someone he loves. He is also not someone without a family. He has co-workers like you. However, because he has not loved God centered on the world and has not resolved the issues of restoration, he cannot avoid walking a lonely path. Even now, he is walking that path.

When will that path end? Even if the teacher's life ends, if that path remains, what will he do? He must still walk it. If you follow that path until you grow old and die but do not fulfill your purpose, what will you do? What will you do? "I will still go." Will you still have to go? "Yes." Because it is the path for the world, it must be walked forever. Because God is eternal, the path of love centered on God cannot be severed. That path is one that must be walked even in death. The spirit world transcends time and space, so even a thousand years in the spirit world is like a day. Therefore, we must think that even if something takes a thousand years to accomplish on this earth, it is the same as accomplishing it in one year.

What kind of path is that? It is the path of true love. Would a parent who truly loves their child forget their child just because ten years have passed since their death? Even if the child's grave has worn down and become level, when the parent visits that grave, they are filled with sorrow that comes from their bones. Isn't that right? They cannot forget until they die.

Even after going to the spirit world, the first thing a parent wants to do is find that child. Wouldn't that be the case? Just because it is hard and difficult does not mean it is forgotten. Just because one ends their own life does not mean it is the end. The inability to fully love centered on a world that can last forever will become a sorrow and a regret for not having poured out one's heart. Living with such a heart is the true form of humanity. The organization that aims to systematize this principle is the Unification Church. Do you understand? "Yes."

Then how should we Unification Church members be? We must become greater than Buddha. We must become greater than Jesus or Confucius. The purpose of religion until now has been to save individuals. However, the Unification Church aims for family salvation rather than individual salvation. This is what differentiates the Unification Church from general religions. It is not about sending the husband to heaven and the wife to hell. It is about both going to heaven. It is also not about sending the mother and father to hell, but about bringing them along and taking the children to heaven as well. The Unification Church teaches the way to take the family one loves, the tribe one loves, to heaven, which is a different dimension from other religions. That is why until now, religions have emphasized single life, but the Unification Church values family. It is centered on the family. That family is a family for the world and for God. This is the path that Unification Church members must follow and the path you must live by in the future.

Loving God and the world more than parents, husbands, wives, and children is the way to be 100% filial to parents, to love husbands 100%, to love wives 100%, and to love children 100%. Since there is no other way to reach a place of value greater than that love, we must walk this path. This path is a common path that all people must walk, and when we walk this path and raise the flag of victory, we will become princes and princesses of heaven who can unify the world and embrace it in our hearts. Therefore, we must clearly understand that this is the path that the members of our Unification Church must walk.

Only those who love others more than themselves can be called true humans. We must have a heart that loves the Republic of Korea more than the Unification Church, a spirit that loves the world more than the Republic of Korea, and a heart that loves the spirit world and future generations more than this world. This is the path that Unification Church members must walk, and we must clearly understand this. Do you understand? "Yes."

<Prayer> Father, today I briefly spoke about the path that Unification Church members must walk, centered on the Unification Church members in the Chuncheon district headquarters in Gangwon Province. 

In order for us to navigate this tremendous path of restoration, we must fight with our lives dedicated to this lifelong mission, so please help us to keep our hearts aligned on this path. If we understand your will, we will know how great and tremendous this path is, but there are still those who do not know it, so I earnestly hope and wish that you grant them the perception and wisdom to understand. 

We know that you wish to fulfill the holy mission of establishing a motherland to represent your eternal world through this pitiful land of Korea and the pitiful delivering nation. Although this fact may not be revealed now, before flowers bloom and leaves sprout, life is already stirring beneath the ground. Those who pass by or merely look on do not realize this fact."
I do not know, but when the autumn season arrives, with the green leaves sprouting and flowers blooming, and fruits bearing, 
I will know everything. 
Today, the autumn season is approaching in the religious world globally. Considering that our Unification Church has the potential to innovate this society and transform it into a true society, it is becoming evident that an environment is emerging where both ourselves and others can recognize this fact. 
As I reflect on how much blood and tears your beloved sons and daughters have shed during this time, 
I realize that your son standing here did not come out for personal glory. I understood how difficult the path you walked was, and I felt deeply that I was unfaithful, unable to meet you with my collar turned down. Every time I feel that I am a lacking person who cannot complain even when I enter a place where I am scorned and trampled upon, I know well that you are with me. 
Father, if there are sons and daughters here whom you must love, and if I have sons and daughters whom I cannot help but love, do you not wish to present them to love the world, and do you not want to see that? What kind of position is it to present beloved children as such sons and daughters? That position is at the crossroads of life and death, a place where the right to life must transcend and leave traces of your love. When I think of this, I earnestly ask that you allow sons and daughters who can move toward such a position to appear here today. 
It is not important to see the face of the teacher, nor is it important to hear the teacher's words, but it is important to live for the purpose that the teacher wishes to leave on this earth. When the world cannot depart from them and God cannot depart from them, may they come to know that God is their God and the world is their world. 
Knowing that love is the only privilege that can bind us so tightly that we cannot be separated, let your sons and daughters become those who are deeply moved by humanity and heavenly feelings, and may they become your sons and daughters who, with utmost sincerity and effort, are determined to love God and the world. 
I earnestly wish and hope that you will personally join us in the event taking place in Tokyo today. What we pray for is that Japan becomes a brotherly nation connected by one blood, not a nation of enemies, and that we must create a way for their concerns to resonate with our concerns. We understand that this cannot be done without centering on you, and we earnestly ask that you fulfill your wishes and establish a new Asia. 
To do this, we have realized that Japan and Korea must unite to absorb China, and we have planned such internal operations without others knowing. All these things must not bring sorrow of defeat before you, but must become matters of glory in victory that we can boast of before all people. 
When the many representatives gathered from around the world finish the conference and return, may they leave behind tears of connection on Japanese soil and form connections that they cannot help but think of in some way. Father, I earnestly wish and hope for this. 
Just as butterflies and bees come to the garden in spring, may all lives in the world be able to connect through that relationship. 
I know that the deep roots of the Unification Church have not yet appeared. May the Victory Alliance stand at the forefront of pioneers on behalf of God's glory and be able to bear the path of all struggles, and may they be moved solely by the single-mindedness of loving the world and loving God. 
Until the day comes when such a movement can move Asia and the world, and you can sit and govern with your command, all must go forth with an indomitable spirit. I earnestly ask that you make your sons and daughters, united in such resolution, run the path of struggle toward the destination. 
Please watch over this time today, and after this time, I earnestly ask that you protect us and personally oversee and guide us. I offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
